City Party Headquarters Prepares for Purification Celebration 104

This Month's 12th Day

In the 13th year of the Republic of China, when the Chinese Nationalist Party held its first national congress, the Chinese Communist Party sent representatives to contact Sun Yat-sen, the General Manager of the Nationalist Party, stating that the Communist Party's past political beliefs were completely wrong and that the Chinese revolution could only succeed by adhering to the Three Principles of the People and the Five-Power Constitution and striving diligently. Therefore, all members of the Communist Party would withdraw from the Communist Party and would join the Nationalist Party as individuals. Sun Yat-sen, the General Manager of the Nationalist Party, believed that the members of the Communist Party were mostly young and that their temporary mistakes were forgivable, so he allowed them to join in their individual capacity. However, the cunning and treacherous Communists, after joining the Nationalist Party, saw that General Manager Sun was alive and did not dare to engage in rampant usurpation. After the General Manager went north and passed away, they engaged in discord and alienated the loyal comrades of the Nationalist Party. They then usurped the cadres and seized key positions. All comrades who were loyal to the Three Principles of the People were either forced into exile or destroyed on some pretext. When the Nationalist Party swore to launch the Northern Expedition, the Communists initially engaged in open slander and opposition. Later, they secretly sent confidants to infiltrate the military, hoping to subvert the Nationalist Party and destroy the National Revolution. After the Northern Expeditionary Army recovered Jiangsu and Zhejiang, their intentions became clearer and their plans became more urgent. The members of the Central Committee, Chiang Kai-shek, Wu Zhihui, and Li Shizeng, realized that a crisis was lurking and was imminent, so they decisively took extraordinary measures to carry out the Purification in the 16th year of the Republic of China, which stabilized the foundation of the Party and the nation. Now, the Communist elements within the Nationalist Party have been purged, but the remaining Red Bandits are still harassing the provinces of Fujian, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei. After pacifying the Yan Feng warlords, the Central Government sent a large army to encircle and suppress the bandits and appointed Comrade He Yingqin to act as the Commander-in-Chief to be responsible for the suppression. The large army is gathering, and the people are cheering. It is certain that they will be able to return victoriously before the National Congress on May 5th. However, recalling the suffering of the people under the Red Bandits and the danger of the Communist Party's attempt to usurp the Party and the nation, we cannot help but feel deeply saddened. On the fourth anniversary of the Purification, we feel even more deeply the greatness and importance of the Purification. The Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special City Party Headquarters has drafted commemorative measures and submitted them to the Municipal Executive Committee for deliberation. The Municipal Executive Committee has now passed the measures. It is reported that a commemorative meeting will be held at 8:00 AM on April 12th in the grand auditorium on the third floor of the City Party Headquarters. At that time, all agencies, organizations, and schools in the city should send four representatives to participate. Pudong, Jiangwan, Wusong, Meilong, Zhenru, and other places that are farther away from the city may convene nearby people separately to hold commemorative ceremonies. On that day, all levels of Party headquarters and permanent propaganda teams will also be dispatched to conduct propaganda.

Conference on Promoting Weights and Measures Postponed 113

City Chamber of Commerce Proposes Supplementary Measures

The Shanghai City Social Affairs Bureau yesterday sent letters to relevant agencies and organizations regarding the promotion of the new system of weights and measures. "To: The writer hereby informs you that the bureau had previously scheduled a meeting on the 12th of this month to discuss the promotion of the new system of weights and measures and has already sent a letter to you for your information. As that day falls on a Sunday holiday, it is feared that the representatives will not be able to attend as scheduled. Therefore, the meeting has been rescheduled to 3:00 PM on Monday, the 13th of this month, still at the Hu'an Building, 8th floor, to discuss everything. This letter is sent for your information." The City Chamber of Commerce had previously convened a meeting of representatives from various industries to discuss the implementation of the new system of weights and measures and resolved six measures. Yesterday, it submitted two supplementary measures to the Social Affairs Bureau for consideration. The measures are recorded below: "(1) In addition to being stamped by the Inspection Office, each new instrument should also be stamped by the respective industry association to facilitate identification. The respective industry associations are responsible for forwarding the instruments to all stores, whether they are members of the association or not, to facilitate statistics. (2) The practice of stores directly submitting new instruments to the Inspection Office for inspection should be prohibited. Instead, the instruments should be collected by the respective industry associations and submitted in batches for inspection to save trouble and avoid variations in style."

United States Increases Import Tax Rate on Egg Products 115

City Chamber of Commerce Cables Ministry of Foreign Affairs to Strive

The City Chamber of Commerce cabled the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing: "To the Ministry of Foreign Affairs in Nanjing, This month, we received a letter from the Egg Factory Association stating that, according to a report in the Zi Lin Daily, and also a cable from a fellow provincial in the United States, the United States Department of Agriculture has a proposal to increase the import tax rate on Chinese egg yolk and egg white, from 18 cents per pound to 27 cents. Chinese egg yolk and egg white have been sold to the United States for decades. The price per pound is only slightly more than 20 cents. These goods are not luxury items. The original tax rate, which is close to 100% of the value, is already excessive. The new rate, which is nearly 150% of the value, is even more outrageous. The intention is nothing more than to limit the import of foreign goods in order to develop domestic agricultural products. Because of the commercial treaty, they cannot openly advocate for boycotts, so they set this strange and harsh tax rate to make Chinese businessmen retreat. In this way, they can avoid the bad name of boycotts and achieve the practical effect of boycotts. The design is skillful and the means are ruthless. The various products of China's egg factory industry have always relied on foreign countries as the only sales channel. Once they are hit by this, the sales channel will be blocked and there will be no other options besides closing down. Not only will the decades of hard work of the industry be completely destroyed, but also hundreds of thousands of workers who rely on it for food and clothing will lose their jobs. Therefore, we urge your office to immediately cable the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and ask the Minister to the United States to directly lodge a strong protest with the President of the United States, urging them to cancel the proposal and reduce the original tax rate to comply with the principle of equality and reciprocity. We are anxiously waiting for your orders." The City Chamber of Commerce stated that the new revised customs import tax rate in China this year, according to American newspapers, is said to have increased but not significantly and does not hinder the flow of American goods, which is comforting. Trade between the two countries must practice the principle of equality and reciprocity in order to increase mutual benefits. The current global market is sluggish, partly due to the strict tariff barriers. The United States' prior efforts to help its many workers are no longer sufficient for politicians. The Far East market serves as a tailpipe for adjustment. If Chinese goods are excluded and taxes are repeatedly increased, it will not be beneficial to US-China trade. Please cable Minister Wu this intention and ask him to present it to the US government earnestly so that they can cancel the tax increase in order to maintain their commercial interests in China, which is in the public interest for manufacturers. The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce respectfully submits this request.

Business Tax Should Be Paid for Concurrent Operation of Brokerage Houses 116

Notice from the County Finance Bureau

The Shanghai County Finance Bureau issued a notice yesterday, which read: "Regarding the matter of notice, according to the instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, concerning the provincial brokerage tax, which is dedicated to education funds, it has been approved to continue to be handled as before. However, upon investigation of the regulations for brokerage houses, the scope is limited to buying and selling on behalf of customers. If, in addition to buying and selling on behalf of customers, there is concurrent self-operated commerce directly selling goods, the concurrent sales portion should still follow the business tax regulations, apply for a business license, and pay business tax, in order to prevent taking advantage and covering up. In addition to separate instructions, it is hereby ordered that the director of the bureau comply with and handle accordingly. Therefore, this notice is issued to all brokerage houses in the county. If the businesses, in addition to buying and selling on behalf of customers, have concurrent self-operated commerce directly selling goods, the concurrent sales portion should still follow the business tax regulations, apply for a business license, and pay business tax, and must not take advantage or cover up, lest they be penalized. This notice is urgent."

Various Industries Request Correction of Business Tax Rates 117

New Pharmaceutical Industry: The New Pharmaceutical Industry Association telegraphed the Executive Yuan of the National Government, the Ministry of Industry, the Ministry of Health, and the Ministry of Finance yesterday regarding the issue of business tax rates, stating that the association had previously requested the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and the Tax Rules Research Committee of various trade associations to telegraph the government to request correction of the tax rate stipulated for the new pharmaceutical industry in the business tax regulations formulated by Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, which exceeded the general principles promulgated by the Ministry. Subsequently, they received a reply stating, "The business tax rate should not exceed two per thousand, unless the government has other regulations stipulating less than two per thousand." The Ministry of Finance has been directly telegraphed, requesting correction during the amendment of the business tax regulations of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and successive instructions have been received, all stating that efforts should be made to ensure that the tax system benefits both commerce and the government. The intentions are greatly appreciated. However, upon recently seeing reports that the Ministry of Finance (your ministry) amended the business tax regulations of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, stipulating two per thousand for traditional Chinese medicine and five per thousand for new medicine, we are greatly alarmed. We believe that medicine is for treating diseases and is greatly related to the lives of the people. It is neither a luxury item nor subject to prohibition. If five per thousand is levied, it not only violates Article 4 of the general principles promulgated by the Ministry but also hinders the improvement of northern-made medicine, which contradicts the Ministry's orders. The Ministry of Health, in view of the rapid development of science, is concerned that old medicines will no longer be improved and wants to eliminate them with the trend of the world. Therefore, there has been a clear order to improve old medicines. New pharmaceutical industries in various places are setting up pharmaceutical factories, adopting traditional Chinese medicine science, and chemically manufacturing new medicines to resist imported goods. If the tax rates levied on traditional Chinese medicine and new medicine are different, it is tantamount to deliberate discrimination. To take a step back, if it is thought that new medicines contain foreign-made medicines, then traditional Chinese medicines also contain imported raw materials. Medicine is mainly for saving people and is more important than food. Even if there are imported goods, it is because there are no such products in the country, and it is unavoidable for the sake of the people's lives. Its tax rate should not be increased. Article 7 of the supplementary measures to the general principles of business tax clearly stipulates that all kinds of business taxes, regardless of whether they operate in domestic or foreign goods, should be taxed at the same tax rate. Therefore, in terms of both reason and law, new medicines and traditional Chinese medicines should be taxed at the same rate. It is reasonable to telegraph your government to instruct (your office to consult) the Ministry of Finance, to take into account the prestige of the government, to consider the pain of pharmaceutical merchants, to correct the business tax rate of new medicines, and not to exceed two per thousand. This would be a great virtue. Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association respectfully bows.

Eyeglasses Industry: The Shanghai Eyeglasses Industry Association was originally organized in the 18th year of the Republic of China as the "Chinese Eyeglasses Association". Now, because it is inconsistent with the laws of the Industrial and Commercial Trade Association, it was initiated by companies such as Daming, Sino-American, Oriental, Jingyi, Jinghua, Xinghua, Central, Dahua, Yaoxiangren, and other companies to reorganize and rename it the Shanghai Eyeglasses Industry Association, in order to comply with laws and regulations and to emphasize public affairs. It is reported that the association has been very perfect since its reorganization. Yesterday, due to the excessive business tax rate, it specifically sent a letter to the Shanghai Tax Rules Research Association of various industries, requesting it to forward the correction, in order to reduce the burden. The original letter is recorded as follows: "Respected Sirs, since the government established business tax to remedy the loss of tariff cuts, the formulation of tax rates in Jiangsu Province, although there is a distinction between the two amounts of business capital, the meaning of the text from one to twelve to twenty has room for activity. The intention is nothing more than to reduce taxes on practical products and increase taxes on luxury goods. The scope of increasing taxes includes the nature of prohibition, and the types of reducing taxes contain the enthusiasm of promotion. The law is perfect. However, for material categories, it is appropriate

Page 10

To strictly distinguish them, so as not to mix luxury and practical use, and to prevent the inappropriateness of increasing and decreasing taxes. This is the reason why your association was organized and established. Because the world has always lacked considerable research on our industry, there are many people who regard it as a luxury item, and there are also many who regard it as a practical item, which makes the government's current regulations on the business tax rate of the eyeglasses industry unable to balance with the lumber tax rate (the Ministry of Finance amended the business tax regulations of Jiangsu Province, stipulating two per thousand for lumber and ten per thousand for eyeglasses). We dare to briefly state our humble opinion for your association's adoption. Although there are only three types of eyeglasses: nearsighted, farsighted, and plano, each has a special function. For example, people with nearsightedness mostly cannot see far away. Once they wear nearsighted glasses, everything that is far away is immediately presented in front of them. Elderly people with depleted essence and blood and lack of vision often find it difficult to read newspapers and write. Once they wear farsighted glasses, the subtle details are immediately distinguishable, and they can read and write freely. All young people who are eager to study should know that prolonged vision can most easily injure the blood. Wearing plano glasses often not only has hygienic benefits but also contains the function of protection. As for colored glasses, they can block sunlight and lamplight, and are most suitable for sick eyes, with the function of treatment. From this point of view, it can be seen that eyeglasses are to the eyes as medicine is to disease. Therefore, many European and American countries list eyeglasses as medicinal items, which can be said to be very appropriate. Before the business tax rate of Shanghai City has been approved by the Ministry, please ask your association to forward the correction of the business tax rate of our industry. Our industry is very fortunate."

The National Federation of Match Industries recently received letters from members in various places, stating that when transporting matches and paying unified taxes, or when the matches are exposed to moisture during the journey, the companies will re-transport all or part of the matches in order to maintain their credit. City Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Ministry of Finance to Request Correction of Foil Industry Special Tax 120

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday to request correction of the special business tax for the foil industry. The original text reads: "To the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, on the 9th of this month, we received a letter from the Foil Industry Association stating that on the 4th, we received a letter from your association stating that we received an electrical message from the Ministry of Finance stating that according to the reply from the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance, the special business tax for the foil industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang is levied according to the original special tax plan, and the tax revenue is used to fund Zhejiang's administrative expenses, and a portion is allocated to prepare for the livelihood of foil workers, and the remaining amount is allocated to the central government and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, totaling more than 500,000 yuan per year, and the Jiangsu Provincial Government is consulted that the sale of Zhejiang foil in Jiangsu Province will no longer be subject to other taxes, so as to avoid double burden, in order to comply with the original intention of the order of the Academy to handle the case. The recording of the electrical message has been delivered, and we hope to check it. Upon investigation, the special business tax for foil in Jiangsu and Zhejiang has been allocated to the central education fund under the original plan, with 300,000 yuan per year for Jiangsu and 270,000 yuan for Jiangsu. The Jiangsu Provincial Government is consulted that the sale of Zhejiang foil in Jiangsu will no longer be subject to other taxes. Why does the Shanghai Customs always refuse to report on the new tax bills issued by Zhejiang Province? Since the beginning of this year, when Zhejiang foil is shipped from Ningbo to Shanghai, or from Shanghai to various counties in northern Jiangsu, when passing through the customs, the new tax bills are generally invalid. Unless taxes are paid again, they will not be released. This is inconsistent with the original plan, and we earnestly request the Ministry of Finance to correct it. Second, during the former special tax era, after one tax was paid, it could pass through the whole country, and the checkpoints were inspected and released without any difficulty. Now, the original plan submitted by Zhejiang Province to the Ministry specifies that the sales area is limited to Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and the scope is too narrow, which hinders sales. We have already felt the pain of not being able to circulate. Unexpectedly, in fact, even within the two provinces, it cannot pass without hindrance, and customs duties must be paid again, which directly troubles the business of foil merchants and indirectly hinders the livelihood of foil workers. This is inconsistent with the original plan, and we earnestly request the Ministry of Finance to correct it. In summary, the foil merchants feel very painful. Recently, we read in the newspaper that the National Government is planning to levy a special tax or registration tax on tin foil. If it is as reported, it will inevitably be taxed repeatedly. The foil merchants are weak and cannot bear the heavy burden. Our association is extremely panicked. For this reason, we urgently present this letter, and we respectfully request your association to appreciate our sincerity and provide assistance, and allow us to telegraph the Ministry of Finance, to consider the difficulties of merchants, and not to increase the burden of foil merchants, implement a one-item-one-tax system, and allow it to pass through the whole country. And we request the customs in various places to exempt the Zhejiang foil from customs duties according to the old case, and still verify and release it with the new tax bill, in order to maintain the livelihood of the foil industry. Upon investigation, when the foil industry was handling the special tax, it was only worth 12.5 per hundred. This time, it was changed to a special business tax, and it is reported that it is worth 5 per thousand. Although the original text of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Finance stated that it was still taxed according to the old rate, in fact, it has exceeded it. Moreover, after the special tax was collected in full in the past, it was able to pass through the whole country, but this time it is limited to the scope of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and it is also said that no other taxes will be levied separately, and the Shanghai Customs always refuses to verify and release the new tax bills issued by Zhejiang Province, and it will not be released unless another tax is paid. All these are inconsistent with the original plan. Such repeated taxation will inevitably erode the lifeline of the foil industry. It is reasonable to telegraph the Ministry of Finance to review and approve it, and to correct it one by one according to the original plan, in order to maintain the livelihood of the industry. In addition, the special business tax paid by the industry, the tax rate is the same as the tax rate of the special consumption tax and the business tax, and the tax revenue is divided between the central government and the local government. Then, no matter what new tax is to be implemented in the future, the industry should be excluded, in order to comply with the general practice of one item one tax. Please also give a clear instruction to avoid the industry's suspicion. Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce."

Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Continues to Submit Application for License 121

The Shanghai Sauce, Wine, Tobacco, and Salt Joint Industry Association, after the members requested the open application for a license, received a reply from the Ministry of Finance, and yesterday submitted a letter to the Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau, Director Guan Wenyun, stating that the letter was submitted for the approval of the Ministry, requesting your office to be sympathetic and approve it, to relieve the difficulties of Jiangsu merchants and to fulfill the expectations of the public. Our association has previously requested the members of the two industries to apply for a license tax openly, and submitted the suffering situation to the Ministry of Finance for verification, and sent representatives to Beijing to petition your office. On the 2nd of this month, we received the Ministry of Finance's printed letter No. 12306, stating that the letter has been received, and the Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau has been ordered to verify and handle it. Our association is deeply grateful for the approval and is deeply impressed by the Ministry of Finance and your office's understanding of the commercial situation and preferential treatment. It is true that the tobacco and alcohol license tax is properly applied by the two industry associations, and the contractor system, which is purely for profit, is a policy that harms merchants. Now, we continue to present the details, investigating the tobacco and alcohol merchants who set up shops for business, and there are no regulations for spending when obtaining a license according to regulations, and the second district tobacco and alcohol license tax office, as a fixed example, charges an additional 1.2 yuan, under the name of application registration fee. For example, the Baoshan branch charges an additional 1.2 yuan for the numbers of the two industries, which is one of the harsh taxes that harms merchants. Furthermore, if the tax is overdue, the provincial regulations stipulate the level, and the office arbitrarily increases it month by month, adding one in the first month, two in the next month, and three in the last month, which is the second harsh tax that harms merchants. All previous tax offices have posted announcements in advance before the collection of each quarter, so that the public knows, and the address is added to the photo, so that merchants can go to the office to pay taxes within the time limit, so as to avoid the pain of additional penalties. In recent years, the tax office has not announced the collection, and the address is not marked, so that merchants cannot find it, and cannot pay within the time limit, which is the third harsh tax that harms merchants. In addition, there are collection personnel who arbitrarily solicit, and there are many malpractices, and small shops are most affected, and there is no recourse. Therefore, when the contracting period is approaching, the merchants of the two industries have requested our association to petition for open application and relieve the pain. The representatives have been convened for many meetings, and they have all paid the tobacco and alcohol license tax by the two industries to avoid the control of outsiders, and decided to submit a petition to pay the Jiangsu second district, the tobacco and alcohol license tax of the entire district, according to the tax amount of the 19th year, and the representatives have personally presented the various sections, and the monarch has adopted them, and the gratitude is indescribable. In view of the Ministry's instructions, it is reasonable to submit a letter for the sequel, and request your office to be considerate of the difficulties of the merchants, and quickly approve it, in order to comply with public opinion, and be grateful for the opportunity to wait. Sincerely presented to Director Guan of the Jiangsu Stamp Tax Bureau.

Customs Clearance Industry Strike City Social Bureau Mediates 122

Summoning Both Parties for Questioning Today

The customs clearance workers in this city went on strike on the 6th because the Cotton Cloth Industry Association cancelled the cotton cloth freight and inspection fees, and the transportation of cotton cloth and yarn was completely stopped, affecting the shipping and causing panic among the customers. Yesterday, five workers of the inspection team were arrested. The authorities decided to summon them for questioning today in order to mediate. The details of the various situations are recorded as follows:

Workers Arrested: The day and night shift inspection team organized by the Customs Clearance Industry Union, as usual, went out to inspect yesterday. The night shift fifth team members Wang Ahe, Cheng Pinshun, and others, at about 6 pm, discovered that Xiexiang Public Firm was smuggling fifteen packages of sixteen Tianguan cotton yarn at the Taikoo Wharf, and immediately detained them. The two sides clashed. The matter was known to the French Patrol Room, and the patrol was dispatched to detain the goods along with the five inspectors and the smugglers at the Sixteen Shop Patrol Room. The union, upon hearing the news, immediately asked lawyer Fan Gang to negotiate, and at the same time sent someone to Xiexiang Public Firm for serious negotiations.

Authority Mediation: The City Social Bureau, because of the strike of customs clearance workers, the suspension of cotton yarn and cloth transportation, has a significant impact on social security and the business community. In order to quickly resolve the situation, in addition to sending someone to investigate the truth, it also designated a commissioner to summon both the Customs Clearance Industry Union and the Cotton Cloth Industry Association to the bureau at 2 pm today to listen to the questioning, in order to mediate and avoid the expansion of the labor movement.

Yarn Industry Panic: The Cotton Yarn Industry Market, for the cotton yarn suspension problem, yesterday sent a letter to the Customs Clearance Industry Union, stating that it was responding to your letter, I have learned, and I have also received a letter from my colleagues, deeply saddened by the strike of your union's staff. This matter is related to the Cotton Cloth Industry's proposal to cancel the car force. It is completely unrelated to my colleagues in the textile industry. The suspension of the loading and transportation of yarn and cloth will inevitably affect my colleagues in the textile industry. Moreover, the registration of old goods ends on April 15th. If it expires, a unified tax will be added. If there are disputes and losses between my colleagues and the customers in the future, your union will not be able to avoid the blame. Not only that, but the price of cotton yarn fluctuates from time to time. If the date is extended, more disputes will inevitably arise. If the customers are eager to load and transport, and entrust the foreign company to handle it, your industry will also feel disadvantaged. Therefore, I specifically inform you that the cotton yarn item should be restored to the loading and transportation work first. Not only will my colleagues avoid accidental losses, but your industry will also have a deep concern.

Union General Meeting: The Customs Clearance Industry Union held a joint emergency board meeting at 2 pm yesterday. Fourteen directors and supervisors, including Sun Dongsheng, attended. He Yumin presided over the meeting. It was resolved that (1) Su Houren, Xin Xiang, Li Houfu, He Yumin, He Yuqin, Liang Jikang, Zhou Juxing, Sun Dongsheng, and other eight people should attend the City Social Bureau mediation meeting as representatives. (2) Liang Jikang, the director of the investigation department, when attending the mediation meeting, his duties will be represented by Xu Rongsheng. (3) If members of the foreign goods department request to join the strike assistance case, if the Cotton Cloth Industry has no sincerity in accepting mediation, they will be allowed to join on the 13th. Also, regarding the economic issues during the union strike period, the members are very enthusiastic. Each person helps 5 yuan, and 1,600 yuan was received on the spot.

Declaration of Difficult Workers of Chunhua Rubber Factory 124

The difficult workers of Chunhua Rubber Factory issued a declaration yesterday, and the following is an excerpt: Since the factory was burned down on December 23, 19, it has ignored the livelihood of more than 100 workers. After the workers repeatedly pleaded, they were unable to invite their pity. They were forced to apply to the City Social Bureau for mediation. The City Social Bureau mediated and was established on January 15, and the factory provided food until the start date and gave subsidies of 45 cents per person per day. However, the factory did not apply for arbitration during the specified period, and after the application for arbitration period, its true attitude was not clearly expressed. The workers had no choice but to sue the local court. After being summoned by the court, the factory was ordered to provide food first, and other parts were paid for investigation first. Later, the factory suddenly applied to the City Social Bureau for a second mediation. The workers thought that this procedure seemed to have little legal basis, but in order to take care of the feelings of both parties, they were not willing to insist. After the second mediation decision, in addition to maintaining the original state of providing food, all the subsidies of 45 cents per person per day were reduced to 2 cents per person per day. After the decision was made, the factory did not fulfill it, and when the workers applied for it, they instead instructed a large number of ruffians to seek revenge from the workers. The workers then listed the facts and submitted them to the City Public Security Bureau for filing. Since then, the workers have deeply felt that the factory cannot be reasoned with. All the compulsory savings of 5% of the wages and the due holiday wages and bonuses cannot be delayed any longer, so they applied to the City Social Bureau for the return. The City Social Bureau convened two mediations, but it has not been resolved today, and another meeting will be held. The workers lead the way and wait. However, the factory falsely accused the party and government organs, saying that the workers were illegally rioting, and secretly left their confidants, intending to undermine unity, and fortunately the party and government organs were clearly aware and not blinded. The workers' conscience was not destroyed, and they were not incited, and their plan ultimately failed. On the 7th of this month, the factory announced the start of work in advance. The workers heard the news and rushed to the factory to work. However, in addition to forcing the workers to sign and register, the factory also stated in the registration book that each person would receive a registration fee of 1 yuan, and would be paid after going to work, and stated that the registration fee would no longer be issued separately, and it would have to be paid within 4 hours, and no one would be allowed to leave the factory to borrow, and they would be immediately fired if they were overdue. The workers could not remain silent, so they publicly recommended two representatives to send the registration book to the Social Bureau for verification. The Social Bureau representative took the registration book and criticized the factory for excessive demands. The workers were in this environment, thinking of the past, and wanting to shed tears, and they did not know how to solve the problem in the future.

The Haiqi Compatriot Organization Forms a Support Association for Wronged People 127

Yesterday, a moving appeal and declaration were issued to all sectors.

Yu Jingyu and others, fellow villagers from Haimen and Qidong counties residing in Shanghai, recently reported that their hometowns have been subjected to wanton arson and murder by bandits, with executions extending to ten families. The severity of the situation is unprecedented. Consequently, they have established the Haiqi Support Association for Wronged People at Nanhua Public School in Shanghai, seeking assistance from all sectors. The following is their moving appeal and declaration:

Moving Appeal to All Newspaper Offices and All Sectors: Please be aware that our counties, Haimen and Qidong, are located along the river and sea, blessed with abundant resources and prosperous livelihoods. The customs are honest and simple, and doors are not locked at night. During the Taiping Rebellion, families from various provinces sought refuge here, regarding Haimen and Qidong as havens of peace. However, since the dynastic change, natural disasters and man-made calamities have followed one after another. The old and weak fill the ditches, while the young and strong scatter in all directions. Some even resort to banditry due to hunger and cold. However, we have never heard of incidents involving people gathering in groups, armed with weapons, committing murder and robbery. Such events only began after our Party secured the Central Plains and began the suppression of communism. The tragedies have also started simultaneously. Consequently, both old and new evil forces, regardless of the extent of their power, can act perversely, disregarding the National Government's decree to protect human rights. Without legal procedures or evidence, they can arbitrarily carry out arson, murder, and executions based on their whims, fabricating reports. As a result, hundreds of cases have occurred in the past year. Posthumous executions extending to ten families and forced signatures are commonplace, with the number of those punished being ten or a hundred times greater. Their authority is unparalleled. Examining judicial and military law, the conviction and charges must be announced when killing a person, however they disregard this. Thus, under such accumulated power, 1.2 million people live in fear, like cicadas in winter, their lives at the mercy of others. Any resistance results in immediate death. Such cruel and brutal acts are taking place under the banner of the Republic, which is outrageous. We have been living in other places for many years, detached from our hometown affairs. In the past, when victimized families came to us with their grievances, we often dismissed them as deserving of their fate. But, the cycle of revenge has escalated and become more severe. Upon investigation, we found that some were bribed to be killed, others were framed on false charges, and some were burned to death in groups, their abdomens cut open, their hearts dug out, and their genitals burned. Most incomprehensibly, large groups of bandits openly roam the jurisdiction's territory armed daily, yet we have never heard of a single case being solved or a single person being killed. If this continues, not only will everyone be in danger, but what will be the end? It can be said that the gate of hell is continuously adding the souls of wronged spirits, and the census records are dwindling innocent people. Therefore, based on the fearless spirit of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, we resolutely established the Haiqi Support Association for Wronged People at Nanhua Public School in Shanghai. We have hired lawyers, published notices in newspapers, collected evidence, conducted thorough investigations, and submitted reports to the authorities, seeking security for the living and vindication for the dead. We are determined not to confuse right and wrong or prioritize personal gain over public interest. Alas, if this scourge is not eradicated, the people's suffering will not end. We are appealing to all sectors like Qin Ting in the court of Chu, earnestly begging for compassion for the helpless and providing powerful assistance. If this happens, our association will be fortunate, and the 1.2 million people of Haiqi will be fortunate.

Declaration: Our association, commiserating with the 1.2 million fellow villagers of Haimen and Qidong who are being trampled upon by old and new evil forces and living in dire straits, subjected to arson, murder, executions, opening abdomens, digging out hearts, and burning genitals, all at their whim, hereby, based on the National Government's decree to protect human rights, resolutely establishes the Haiqi Support Association for Wronged People. We have hired lawyers to collect evidence and conduct thorough investigations, submitting reports to the authorities for a thorough investigation, acting with impartiality, integrity, and indomitable spirit to seek security for the living and vindication for the dead. We will uphold the spirit of Dr. Sun Yat-sen, willing to sacrifice everything to fight a death match with the old and new evil forces. We will not be swayed by personal feelings, be greedy for money, condone wrongdoings, or abuse public office for private gain, nor will we start strongly and end weakly. Our goal of eliminating the communist bandits and overthrowing the old and new evil forces will not cease. This is our declaration.

The Shanghai Municipal Council Discusses the Issue of Sheltering Beggars 129

A decision was made to first inquire with the Chinese-administered shelter.

The Shanghai Times reports that the problem of beggars in the Public Concession has existed for a long time. The Municipal Council has considered the matter more than once through the Police Department. However, after being driven away, these beggars gradually sneak back, becoming increasingly annoying. The previous Municipal Council also raised the matter for consideration. A member of the committee investigating the beggar problem suggested that the beggar shelters in Zhabei and Nanshi were sufficient to accommodate these beggars. Subsequently, a Chinese council member proposed establishing a shelter in the Concession itself. The Chairman did not agree, fearing that it would attract beggars from neighboring areas. Several council members claimed that with strict management and the provision of work in a self-established shelter, beggars would be deterred from entering the Concession. Ultimately, it was decided to first inquire with the Chinese-administered beggar shelters regarding the conditions for also accepting beggars from the Concession before taking further action.

Shanghai Banks Serve Rural Areas 130

Cooperating with the China International Famine Relief Commission

Pilot Project for Farmers' Loans in Hebei Province

The Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank has recently reached an agreement with the China International Famine Relief Commission to jointly implement a method for agricultural lending, starting with an initial investment of 20,000 yuan. Although a small amount, this marks the first time a Chinese bank has invested in agriculture, opening a new path for agricultural development in our country. The following is an account of this initiative: Since 1923, the China International Famine Relief Commission has promoted rural credit cooperatives in Hebei Province. Over the past eight years, cooperatives have been established in various counties, numbering over a thousand. Loans totaling over 220,000 yuan have been issued. Despite the absence of collateral, due to the high credit rating of each cooperative, there has not been a single loss. The reason for this success lies in the commission's pragmatism and the honesty and reliability of the farmers in Hebei. However, the commission's primary mission is disaster relief, and the funds available for cooperative ventures are limited. This type of economic assistance is crucial for agricultural development, and it is difficult to achieve long-term development without involving the financial sector. This spring, Chen Guangfu, the General Manager of the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, traveled north and learned about the current state of rural credit cooperatives in Hebei. He believed that the opportunity to participate in agricultural development with tangible resources had arrived. He instructed Jin Zhongfan, the bank's parallel manager, to negotiate with the Famine Relief Commission. Recently, both parties signed a contract, with the following key points: (1) Assisting the commission in carrying out rural cooperative projects; (2) The loan amount will be based on the cooperative's assessment grade; (3) An initial allocation of 20,000 yuan will be entrusted to the commission for a pilot project, with future expansion planned; (4) The interest rate will be in accordance with the commission's regulations. It is reported that this cooperation agreement has already been implemented.

More local news can be found on the following page.

Account of Li Hefei's Son Narrowly Escaping Danger 131

The kidnappers made extensive prior arrangements.

They intended to act on the road.

He managed to escape by driving away quickly.

His Russian bodyguard was shot and injured.

Li Jingmai, son of Li Hongzhang of Hefei, was almost kidnapped on Hart Road yesterday morning. Fortunately, the car driver was quick-witted and drove away rapidly amidst the sound of smoke bombs, thus avoiding the danger. The bandits fired three shots, one hitting the windshield and two hitting the Russian bodyguard. They then drove away in a car that had been waiting nearby. The injured Russian was sent to the hospital for treatment and his life is feared to be in danger.

The flowers and trees are lush in the Pillow Stream Villa.

Li Jingmai is well-known in Shanghai for his real estate business. Brookside Apartments at 333 Hart Road is his innovative project. This building, known as the Pillow Stream Apartments in Chinese, is elegant and poetic. The towering buildings and summer pavilions are magnificent and unprecedented. Li resides in what he calls the Pillow Stream Villa, located west of the apartments at No. 441. The flowers and trees are lush, resembling a garden. Though called a villa, it is actually a grand structure. Li has long been targeted by criminals and always travels with a Russian bodyguard. Yesterday morning around 9:30, he drove out in his car, No. 244. He returned around 10:45 after running errands. His car was coming from Rue Massenet. Near the intersection of Route Tenant de la Tour and Rue Amiral Bayle, he suddenly saw a collapsed cart blocking the way. One person was pulling while another was pushing, seemingly helping each other. Li's driver, Pavlov, immediately braked to wait for them to pass.

Encountering Kidnappers on the Road, the Bodyguard Injured

The collapsed cart, as it turned out, was a bundle of bamboo poles lying across the road, making it extremely inconvenient to pass. The movements of the two people pushing and pulling were also very slow. Suddenly, a gunshot was heard from behind the car. A bullet hit the car window, shattering the windshield. Then, another bullet hit the Russian bodyguard, Kosnai Chofu, in the shoulder. Kosnai stood up in pain, and a third bullet came from behind, hitting him in the lower waist. At this point, Li realized the situation was dire and ordered the driver, Pavlov, to drive away. Pavlov obeyed and sped off westward. The bandits continued to fire shots at the car from behind, but none hit their target.

Injuries to Vital Areas, Life in Danger

Li returned home and immediately called the police, who dispatched armed detectives to search the scene. However, the bandits had already fled. According to eyewitnesses, the bandits escaped in a car that had been waiting nearby, with the license plate number 1852. The injured Russian bodyguard, Kosnai Tafu, was taken to the Lester Chinese Hospital in a sick car for treatment. Although the bullets had been removed, he had lost too much blood and his injuries were in vital areas, making his life uncertain.

A Collapsed Cart with Twelve Bamboo Poles

Li Jingmai's residence at 441 Hart Road is located in the French Concession, while the incident occurred in the Public Concession. Afterwards, the Jing'an Temple Police Station dispatched detectives to investigate. The number of kidnappers in this case is estimated to be five. The people pushing and pulling the collapsed cart were undoubtedly accomplices. The collapsed cart was very large, but it only carried twelve bamboo poles, which, when measured, were just long enough to block the street. Therefore, it is known that the bandits used this to obstruct Li's car.

Mr. Li Guochao's Account

According to Li's son, Mr. Li Guochao, who spoke to reporters, his father's outings are never fixed, and he always has a bodyguard with him to protect him in case of emergency. Recently, the Russian bodyguard asked for leave, so Kosnai Tafu replaced him. This morning, when accompanying his father, he did not carry a handgun. Because the incident happened suddenly, there was no way to deal with it. Being forced to do so, they could only drive away at full speed. When the bandits fired, the driver, Pavlov, wanted to draw his gun to fight back, but his father stopped him.

The Kidnappers' Plot Was Not a Day Old

Li Jingmai's reputation has attracted the attention of kidnappers for some time. Similar kidnapping attempts have occurred no less than four or five times. The most notable incident occurred last autumn when Li ordered his driver to deliver a letter. When returning, near the Red Cross Hospital on Route Tenant de la Tour, a car suddenly sped out of a side street. There were six bandits in the car, and they were disappointed to see that Li's car was empty. However, threatening letters are received frequently.

The Family Situation of Li Jingmai

Li Jingmai, courtesy name Jigao, is 56 years old and the fourth son of Li Hongzhang. His eldest brother, Jingfang, courtesy name Boxing, currently resides in Tianjin. His other brothers have passed away. Li Jingmai served as an envoy to Austria during the Qing Dynasty, making a name for himself in his official career. After the dynastic change, he became a resident of Shanghai, specializing in real estate. He has many friends, and Westerners often address him as "Lord" to show respect for his ancestor's achievements. Li's son, Li Guochao, courtesy name Dinghou, is married and lives with his father in the Pillow Stream Villa. "Young master and old nobleman" can be used to describe the Li family.

Parents' Orders and Matchmaker's Words End a Daughter's Life 132

Pitiful Xiuying, after taking poison,

Sat silently, tears falling like rain.

Treatment was unsuccessful, and her life was extinguished.

Eight suicide notes, filled with sadness.

A certain Mr. Mo, residing at No. 22, Lane 3, Lao Tianxiang Li, Rue Amiral Courbet in the French Concession, has four sons and three daughters, with a modest family fortune. Except for the youngest son, all are employed in society. The third daughter is married to a Mr. Ma. The eldest daughter is still unmarried. The second daughter, Xiuying, is 23 years old and a literate female student. Her parents, seeing her studious nature, quiet personality, and intelligence beyond ordinary people, loved her dearly. However, ten years ago, based on her parents' orders and the matchmaker's words, she was betrothed to the eldest son of the Wang family in Minhang. However, the Wang household was also an old-fashioned family, and the eldest son was pedantic and unable to understand worldly affairs. On the night before last (the 7th), around 9 pm, she suddenly had a suicidal thought and secretly took poison. After taking the poison, she went upstairs with her younger brother and sat silently. Her brother was reading beside her and initially did not notice anything unusual. After a while, he suddenly saw that his sister's face was abnormal and tears were streaming down her face. He tried to comfort her, but she did not respond and continued to cry. Around 12 o'clock, he saw that his sister's face had turned pale, and her eyes seemed dull. Her tears had gradually dried up. He finally realized something was wrong and told his mother, who immediately ordered a servant to take her to the hospital for treatment. However, all four hospitals said they could not save her and had to bring her home. Before she arrived home, her life was extinguished, and she left the world forever. The funeral was held yesterday morning, and the coffin was taken out at 3 pm. It is also said that before committing suicide, Xiuying had written eight suicide notes to her brother and close friends, filled with sad words. Everyone who read them felt sorry for her and mourned together.

The Municipal Council Does Not Approve of Buying the Paramount Hotel 133

Yesterday, a special declaration was issued.

Stating several reasons.

The proposal to nationalize the land of the Paramount Hotel in western Shanghai was recently included in the agenda of the foreign taxpayers' annual meeting on the 15th of this month at the request of Mr. Harris, a foreign taxpayer. The Municipal Council yesterday issued a statement on the matter, saying that recently many people have suggested that the Municipal Council should buy the land of the Paramount Hotel, and many have written to newspapers to express their opinions. The land covers an area of 58.593 mu, and the owner is willing to sell it to the Municipal Council for 3.5 million yuan, with the deadline being the 30th of this month. The Municipal Council has carefully considered this proposal. Because this matter is of great public concern and will involve a huge amount of public funds, it is necessary to publish the facts and the attitude of the authorities on this matter. Those who advocate purchasing this land have proposed many uses, but they can be divided into three categories: (1) Moving the municipal government offices to the new site and using the funds obtained from selling the old site to offset the cost of purchasing the new property; (2) Using it as a cultural and social center; (3) Using it as a park or square. Regarding the first point, moving the municipal government offices from the current convenient location in the city center to a new location one and a half miles west will cause significant inconvenience in handling public affairs. This action is unwise, and the buildings where the municipal government offices are currently located can still be used for many years and have plenty of room for expansion. After the Shanghai Electric Power Company moves to its new building on Nanjing Road in October of this year, there will be immediate relief. Furthermore, after the current Central Police Station and fire brigade are demolished and moved to new buildings near Fuzhou Road, even more space will be freed up for considerable expansion and development. The second suggestion is vague. If you want to concentrate administrative and public agencies in one place, the land is too small and the cost is too high. After the Central Police Station and fire brigade move to the new site, the municipal government and library will have plenty of room to build. Whether the Paramount property should be purchased as a park should be considered in conjunction with the broader issue of establishing parks and squares in the concession. Today, the addition of parks and squares in the concession is the most urgent task. However, it is extremely difficult to find a suitable location at a reasonable price. The Municipal Council has proposed forming a committee to develop a large-scale plan for adding parks and squares to meet the needs of all residents in the concession. The northern district has the highest population density and the greatest need, so the Municipal Council decided last summer to add them there first. In the western district, a site of 25 acres has already been purchased and will be used as a park in the future. Therefore, the Municipal Council is now focusing on adding recreational facilities to the densely populated northern and eastern districts. Moreover, it is questionable what the actual benefit of spending 3.5 million taels to purchase the Paramount property would be. Perhaps adding two or three squares in densely populated areas with lower land prices would benefit more of the city's residents. Moreover, from a real estate perspective, the Paramount area is rapidly becoming the area with the highest land prices. The Municipal Council does not recognize its special value as a park, and its existing buildings are completely unsuitable for use as a city hall. In terms of the Municipal Council's financial position, purchasing this property is only a small part of the larger plan to add parks and squares, but the large amount will limit the progress of adding parks in more densely populated areas. The Municipal Council also has to consider education, hospitals, and other needs. Moreover, the Municipal Council's current financial position is somewhat artificial. The low tax rate is entirely due to the sale of the electricity division. Once this money is used up, it will be in a difficult position. Therefore, all non-essential expenditures must be avoided. Purchasing the Paramount property is sufficient to hinder the addition of parks in more densely populated areas, and the estimated annual recurring expenses will increase by 250,000 taels, which will be a powerful factor in promoting future tax increases. Therefore, after careful consideration, the Municipal Council believes that it cannot approve this action and believes that its current financial position is not suitable for frequently adding this huge amount to the budget and hindering the progress of other more urgent plans.

Worth more than 140,000 yuan.

In addition, there were books such as "Sexual History."

Yesterday, the Jianghai Customs burned confiscated opium at Lujiazui in Pudong. The Chief of the Customs Warehouse Transportation Department, a Westerner named Roberts, and the Tax Inspector's interpreter, Ge Yixin, supervised the transportation of confiscated goods, numbered thirty-seven items, across the river with the representative of the Supervisory Office, Yang Chongshi, and more than a dozen Chinese and Western customs officials. The goods were weighed and checked against the account books, and each item was verified. At 9 am, two kilns were lit simultaneously to begin burning. By noon, the burning was completed. A total of 30 dan, 2 jin, and 14 liang of opium from Yunnan, Sichuan, and Persia (i.e., red opium) were destroyed, with an estimated value of 140,954 yuan and 2 jiao and 3 fen. In addition, 2 jin and 13 liang of morphine were destroyed, with an estimated value of 1,447 yuan and 6 jiao, as well as morphine-containing pills and liquids with an estimated value of 1,082 yuan and 8 jiao, and opium paraphernalia with an estimated value of 18 yuan. In addition, there was also a large wooden box containing obscene books such as "Sexual History" and "The True Story of a Rake," as well as prohibited almanacs and blank money orders, which were also burned. More than 400 counterfeit pistols, as well as opium lamps, shades, and pipes, were smashed with sledgehammers by laborers. The above-mentioned contraband items were seized by customs officers on various ships from December 21, 1920 to March 20, 1921. Supervisors from various agencies, including Ye Liangguang from the Songhu Garrison Command, Zhang Yinhuai from the Municipal Government, Ju Zhijing from the Special District Court, Wang Zhizhong from the Local Court, Fan Ander and Duan Zhenfen from the Anti-Drug Association, Director Chen of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, specially dispatched Section Member Lin Tao, and Zhang Mingqin, the Third District Chief, supervised the armed police platoon at the scene. Afterwards, they went to the reception room of the Customs School for refreshments and dispersed.

Xue Baorun's Son-in-Law Also Asks for Provisional Seizure of Xue's Property 135

The court ordered a postponement of seven days for further hearing.

Ordered the defendants to report to the case in person.

Gu Qiaolin and Wang A'mei, concubines of the late paint tycoon Xue Baorun, have successively filed lawsuits in the French court to divide the property. Just as one wave subsided, another wave rose. Recently, Hua Lihou, Xue Baorun's son-in-law, accompanied by his two sons, Yi Hong and Yi Gu, and his daughter, Man Yun, sued his mother-in-law, Sun, and his brothers-in-law, Gan Sheng, Yan Sheng, Jia Sheng, and Gen Sheng, in the French court, demanding the division of the estate. The defendants were not present at yesterday's hearing, and lawyer Lin Yingqing appeared on their behalf, claiming that the notice of this case was only delivered the day before yesterday, which happened to be a holiday, and the defendants had gone out for sightseeing and had not yet returned to Shanghai, requesting an extension for debate. The plaintiff's lawyer stated that the defendants were actually in Shanghai and had not left, and were intentionally avoiding appearing in court. Not only were they absent from this case, but they had consistently avoided appearing in court in other cases. Innocently Assaulted and Humiliated, He Falsely Reported a Robbery 136

The law has a special clause for falsely accusing someone of theft.

Yu Huilin was sentenced to three months in prison.

Boatman Yu Huilin returned to his residence at No. 42, Taian Li, North Fujian Road from Waibu the day before yesterday. As he approached his door, he encountered a rogue named Lu Xiaomaotou. Lu tried to search him, but Yu refused. A conflict ensued, and Lu's accomplices ganged up on him and said that if they met again, they would not spare him. After speaking, they scattered. Yu returned home and, although he felt that he had not been harmed this time, he could not guarantee that they would not seek revenge in the future. Wanting to take preemptive action, he reported to the Huizi Police Station, falsely claiming that he had been surrounded by four or five thieves in Taian Li, including one named Lu Xiaomaotou, who threatened him with a handgun and forbade him from making noise, while the others searched him and robbed him of 5,000 yuan in cash. However, after the chief detective sent investigators, it was discovered that it was a false report motivated by revenge, which is not allowed by law. Yu was arrested and sent to the Special District Local Court yesterday morning, charged with false accusation. Yu also admitted to falsely reporting the robbery, saying that he wanted to scare Lu to prevent him from becoming violent in the future. Judge Ge said that if Yu had been innocently assaulted, he could have reported it to the police truthfully. Instead, he acted impulsively and falsely accused someone of theft, which was a well-deserved crime. Therefore, he immediately sentenced Yu Huilin to three months in prison as a warning.

Mute Love Film Public Lawsuit 137

The Defendant's Lawyer's Six Reasons

Debate Concludes, Verdict in Fifteen Days

Because the Xifan Film Company produced the mute love film on behalf of the Shishi Film Company, involving Wu Airong's stepmother, Wu Yangshi, and her brother, Wu Baolun, Wu Yangshi and others filed a private lawsuit in the local court against Ren Xifan, Chen Zhuomin, Zhang Fukang, and others for insult and defamation. Yesterday, Judge Qian Chengjun continued the hearing. The judge asked Ren Xifan where Ran Zhongfen of the Shishi Film Company had gone. He replied, "Hong Kong and then Nanyang." At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer, Shen Chuqing, requested the court to order Ren's arrest. The judge said, "Since Liang is the nominal defendant, the warrant is valid. Even if the defendant does not appear, a verdict can be rendered. There are ways." The judge questioned the lawyer, "Regarding the indictment against the Shishi Film Company, it only mentions the company's name and not Liang's name, which is not legal." The lawyer stated, "This is a legal entity." The judge said, "In criminal cases, natural persons should be used. In civil lawsuits, legal entities can be used, so the indictment should be supplemented." The lawyer agreed. The judge then asked Ren Xifan, "Regarding Lin Jim and Wu Airong, did you invite them, or did they come voluntarily?" He replied, "They came to the Shishi Company requesting filming. Because Shishi had no venue, they entrusted my company to film it on their behalf." The judge asked, "How many times was it shown in Shanghai?" He replied, "Nine times. Lin and Wu performed on stage at the Guang Stage before coming to film." The judge asked Chen Zhuomin, "Was it for publicity at the Xifan Company?" Chen replied, "Yes, for publicity in newspapers." The judge asked Zhang Fukang, "I was the photographer. The facts inside depended on the instructions of director Chen Zhuomin." The judge asked Wu Yangshi and Wu Baolun, "They requested incidental civil compensation of three thousand taels of silver, to be borne jointly by the two companies." The judge then questioned the defendants, who were unwilling to compensate. At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer, Shen, stated, "In the film, the mute and Airong met through Wu Baolin. The 'Lin' character in Wu Baolin's name sounds the same as 'Lun' in the Cantonese dialect. The plaintiff is Airong's stepmother. The explanation states that Wu Airong could not bear the stepmother's beatings, so she followed Hongfu's elopement. It clearly points to the stepmother driving her away. The successful marriage was also due to Wu Baolin's mediation. This is a serious insult. According to Articles 324, 325, and 328 of the criminal law, Ren Xifan, Chen Zhuomin, and Zhang Fukang should be subject to appropriate criminal penalties. As for Liang Zhongfen of the Shishi Film Company, who has not appeared, we request his arrest. In the civil part, they showed the film, which affected the plaintiffs' personality and reputation, and they should naturally compensate," etc. The defendant's lawyer, Wu Chengyu, stated, "(1) The plaintiff is suing for two crimes, insult and defamation. According to the study of criminal law, one act cannot constitute two crimes. The plaintiff's and the agent's views are already wrong. (2) The defendants do not know the plaintiffs. Lin Jim and Wu Airong wrote out the facts, and the name of the stepmother was not mentioned. In any case, the sounds of Lin and Lun cannot be the same. There is no crime without intentional conduct. (3) Is it a disgraceful thing for Wu Yangshi as a stepmother to beat her son? This is like parents teaching their children. Wu Baolin introduced Lin Jim to Airong and mediated their marriage. According to the new morality, it is a free marriage. According to the old morality, Wu Airong remained faithful to one person until the end, which is not a disgraceful thing. (4) Wu Airong and Lin Jim appeared in court to prove these facts. According to Article 325, those who can prove the facts are not punished. Regarding private morality, a mother beating her daughter is a virtue in the old morality. The film is a news report on old families and has nothing to do with public interest. (5) The plaintiff is a stepmother. If the film is not shown, Airong will have no means of support. Therefore, the child born has to be sent to the hall. Anyone with a conscience would not file a lawsuit. (6) Can the facts in the film be considered a well-intentioned and appropriate comment? Therefore, the public prosecution is innocent, and the private prosecution is naturally not established." At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer stated again, "Ren Xifan claimed that he printed the advertisement, which proves defamation. The defendant's defender said that only one crime can be made. If the defendant's criminal facts are many, the court can only judge one crime, which is too unreasonable. This is an infringement of personal legal rights and has nothing to do with the public. Is women's virtue not related to private morality? Therefore, the film must be requested to be revoked and confiscated. The private lawsuit clearly infringes on the personality of others. According to Article 16 of the civil law, the private lawsuit should not be invalid just because the public prosecution is not established." The defendant's lawyer stated again, "Private morality is private morality that cannot be told to others. Therefore, this issue is still about women's virtue." At this point, the judge announced the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict to be announced at 9:00 a.m. on the 15th of this month. The court adjourned.

New Building of the Shanghai Trust Department of the Continental Bank

In addition to the shops on the three sides of the main road, Wangping Street, and Second Malu Road, the two sides in the middle of the T-shaped road are also arranged with shops, with superior locations and prosperous traffic on three sides. The second, third, and fourth floors are all used as markets, with each storefront having a passage of more than two yards wide, surrounding the area according to the terrain, with access everywhere. The rent is cheaper than the shops downstairs, which is suitable for the needs of medium-capital businesses. From the fifth floor upwards, it is designated as office space. On the Second Malu Road side, it can also be used for apartments. At the entrance on the main road, there are two elevators. At the entrances on Wangping Street and Second Malu Road, there is one elevator each. There are also five or six stone staircases, which can ensure safety. A garden is arranged on the roof for viewing. Iron frames are placed in the high places facing the air, tilted outwards, specifically for installing high-end electric light advertisements. The most meaningful part of the plan is on the Second Malu Road side, where a lane is specially opened to preserve a hotel with historical connections, so that those who love antiquity will not feel a sense of vicissitudes, which shows the department's painstaking efforts in planning. It is heard that this project has already started, and it is expected to be completed by the end of the year. There will be a new atmosphere in the eastern part of the main road.
